Source Code

These source-code files derive from a printout of Luminary 210 (Apollo 15-17 Lunar Module guidance computer program), from the personal library of original AGC developer Don Eyles, digitally photographed at archive.org, financially sponsored by Jim Lawton, and transcribed to source code by a team of volunteers. This colorized, syntax-highlighted form was created by assembling that transcribed source code. Note that the full page images are available on the Virtual AGC project page at archive.org, while reduced-size images are presented at the VirtualAGC project website. Report or fix any transcription errors at the Virtual AGC project code repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 210 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY 
	BY NASA 2021112-161 17:11 MAR. 19,1971
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

017469,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
017470,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
017471,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 210.
017472,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM)
017473,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 15-17.
017474,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
017475,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
017476,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
017477,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
017478,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 402-486
017479,000012:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
017480,000013:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.

017489,000022:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
017490,000023:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
017491,000024:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
017492,000025:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
017493,000026: 
017494,000027:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
017495,000028: 
017496,000029:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
017497,000030:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
017498,000031:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
017499,000032:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
017500,000033:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
017501,000034:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
017502,000035:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
017503,000036:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
017504,000037:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
017505,000038: 
017506,000039:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
017507,000040:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
017508,000041:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
017509,000042:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
017510,000043:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
017511,000044:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
017512,000045: 
017513,000046: 
017514,000047:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
017515,000048: 
017516,000049:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
017517,000050:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
017518,000051:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
017519,000052:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
017520,000053:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017521,000054: 
017522,000055:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
017523,000056:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
017524,000057:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
017525,000058:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017526,000059: 
017527,000060:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
017528,000061:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
017529,000062:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
017530,000063:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
017531,000064:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017532,000065: 
017533,000066: 
017534,000067:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
017535,000068: 
017536,000069:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
017537,000070:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
017538,000071:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS TO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 403 

017540,000073:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
017541,000074:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
017542,000075:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
017543,000076:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
017544,000077:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
017545,000078:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
017546,000079:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
017547,000080:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
017548,000081:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
017549,000082:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
017550,000083: 
017551,000084:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
017552,000085:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
017553,000086:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017554,000087: 
017555,000088: 
017556,000089:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
017557,000090: 
017558,000091:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
017559,000092:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
017560,000093:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
017561,000094: 
017562,000095:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
017563,000096:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
017564,000097:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
017565,000098:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
017566,000099:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
017567,000100:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
017568,000101:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
017569,000102: 
017570,000103:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
017571,000104:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017572,000105: 
017573,000106: 
017574,000107:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
017575,000108: 
017576,000109:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
017577,000110:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
017578,000111:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
017579,000112:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
017580,000113: 
017581,000114: 
017582,000115:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
017583,000116: 
017584,000117:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
017585,000118:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.   REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
017586,000119:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
017587,000120:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
017588,000121: 
017589,000122:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 404 

017591,000124:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
017592,000125: 
017593,000126: 
017594,000127:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
017595,000128: 
017596,000129:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
017597,000130:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
017598,000131: 
017599,000132:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
017600,000133:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
017601,000134:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
017602,000135:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
017603,000136: 
017604,000137:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
017605,000138:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
017606,000139: 
017607,000140:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
017608,000141:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
017609,000142:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
017610,000143:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
017611,000144: 
017612,000145:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
017613,000146:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
017614,000147: 
017615,000148:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
017616,000149:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
017617,000150: 
017618,000151:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
017619,000152: 
017620,000153:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
017621,000154:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
017622,000155:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
017623,000156:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017624,000157: 
017625,000158:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
017626,000159:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017627,000160: 
017628,000161:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
017629,000162:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
017630,000163: 
017631,000164: 
017632,000165:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
017633,000166:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
017634,000167:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.

(Note that this doc by Green and Filene is/was available online at http://www.ibiblio.org/apollo/hrst/archive/1706.pdf --- MAS 11/2016.)

017642,000175:                                                                                                  #  USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

Page 405 

017644,000177:                                                                                                  #  CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
017645,000178: 
017646,000179:                                                                                                  #                       HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
017647,000180: 
017648,000181: 
017649,000182:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
017650,000183: 
017651,000184: 
017652,000185:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017653,000186: 
017654,000187:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT ERASE                  DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
017655,000188:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH ERASE                  +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
017656,000189:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG  ERASE                  VERB CODE
017657,000190:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG  ERASE                  NOUN CODE
017658,000191:                                                                                                  #  XREG     ERASE                  R1 INPUT BUFFER
017659,000192:                                                                                                  #  YREG     ERASE                  R2 INPUT BUFFER
017660,000193:                                                                                                  #  ZREG     ERASE                  R3 INPUT BUFFER
017661,000194:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017662,000195:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017663,000196:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT =      YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017664,000197:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
017665,000198:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017666,000199:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT =      ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017667,000200:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
017668,000201:                                                                                                  #  MODREG   ERASE                  MODE CODE
017669,000202:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK  ERASE                  KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
017670,000203:                                                                                                  #  REQRET   ERASE                  RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
017671,000204:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT ERASE                  STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
017672,000205:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS   ERASE                  PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
017673,000206:                                                                                                  #  NOUT     ERASE                  ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
017674,000207:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR ERASE                  MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
017675,000208:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE  ERASE                  N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
017676,000209:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 ERASE                  NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR(MATBS) =MONSAVE +1
017677,000210:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2 ERASE                  NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017678,000211:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB   ERASE          +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13,C RELAYS
017679,000212:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR ERASE                  ENDIDLE STORAGE
017680,000213:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM   ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
017681,000214:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
017682,000215:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
017683,000216:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVQTEM+1
017684,000217:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE ERASE                  NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
017685,000218:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST  ERASE                  WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
017686,000219:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT ERASE                  EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
017687,000220:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
017688,000221:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
017689,000222:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017690,000223: 
017691,000224: 
017692,000225:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

017694,000227:                                                                                                  #  DSEXIT   =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR DSPIN
017695,000228:                                                                                                  #  EXITEM   =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
017696,000229:                                                                                                  #  BLANKRET =      INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
017697,000230: 
017698,000231:                                                                                                  #  WRDRET   =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK
017699,000232:                                                                                                  #  WDRET    =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR DSPWD
017700,000233:                                                                                                  #  DECRET   =      INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
017701,000234:                                                                                                  #  21/22REG =      INTBIT15        TEMP FOR CHARIN
017702,000235: 
017703,000236:                                                                                                  #  UPDATRET =      POLISH          RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
017704,000237:                                                                                                  #  CHAR     =      POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
017705,000238:                                                                                                  #  ERCNT    =      POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
017706,000239:                                                                                                  #  DECOUNT  =      POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
017707,000240: 
017708,000241:                                                                                                  #  SGNON    =      VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
017709,000242:                                                                                                  #  NOUNTEM  =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
017710,000243:                                                                                                  #  DISTEM   =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
017711,000244:                                                                                                  #  DECTEM   =      VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
017712,000245: 
017713,000246:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF   =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR +,- ON
017714,000247:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP   =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
017715,000248:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1  =      VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART(=SFTEMP2-1)
017716,000249:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN  =      VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017717,000250:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
017718,000251:                                                                                                  #  CODE     =      VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
017719,000252:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2  =      VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART(=SFTEMP1+1)
017720,000253:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN  =      VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017721,000254:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMIN+1
017722,000255:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP  =      VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
017723,000256:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET  =      VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
017724,000257: 
017725,000258:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
017726,000259: 
017727,000260:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET   =      DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
017728,000261: 
017729,000262:                                                                                                  #  WDONT    =      DOTRET          CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
017730,000263:                                                                                                  #  INREL    =      DOTRET          INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR ( X,Y,Z, REG )
017731,000264: 
017732,000265:                                                                                                  #  DSPMMTEM =      MATINC          DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
017733,000266:                                                                                                  #  MIXBR    =      MATINC          INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN
017734,000267:

017736,000269:                                                                                                  #  DSREL    =      TEM1            REL ADDRESS FOR DSPIN

017740,000273:                                                                                                  #  IDADDTEM =      TEM2            MIXNOUN INDIRECT ADDRESS STORAGE

017743,000276:                                                                                                  #  COUNT    =      TEM3            FOR DSPIN

017759,000292:                                                                                                  #  IDAD1TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)

017765,000298:                                                                                                  #  RUTMXTEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN ONLY)
017766,000299:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017767,000300: 
017768,000301: 
017769,000302:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017770,000303: 
017771,000304:                                                                                                  #  MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
017772,000305:                                                                                                  #  BUF, +1, +2
017773,000306:                                                                                                  #  BUF2, +1, +2
017774,000307:                                                                                                  #  MPTEMP
017775,000308:                                                                                                  #  ADDRWD
017776,000309:                                                                                                  #    END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
017777,000310: 
017778,000311: 
017779,000312:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
017780,000313: 
017781,000314:                                                                                                  #  DSPCNT   ERASE                  COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
017782,000315:                                                                                                  #  UPLOCK   ERASE                  BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
017783,000316:                                                                                                  #                                                                          RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
017784,000317:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
017785,000318: 
017786,000319: 
017787,000320:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
017788,000321: 
017789,000322:                                                                                                  #  KEYTEMP1 =      WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
017790,000323:                                                                                                  #  DSRUPTEM =      WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
017791,000324:                                                                                                  #  KEYTEMP2 =      RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
017792,000325:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
017793,000326:

Page 408 

017795,000328:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
017796,000329:                                                                                                  #  0        10000
017797,000330:                                                                                                  #  1        00001
017798,000331:                                                                                                  #  9        01001
017799,000332:                                                                                                  #  VERB     10001
017800,000333:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES10010
017801,000334:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE 11001
017802,000335:                                                                                                  #  +        11010
017803,000336:                                                                                                  #  -        11011
017804,000337:                                                                                                  #  ENTER    11100
017805,000338:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR    11110
017806,000339:                                                                                                  #  NOUN     11111

(2003 RSB -- The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism.) 

017808,000341: 
017809,000342: 
017810,000343:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
017811,000344:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
017812,000345:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
017813,000346:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
017814,000347:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
017815,000348:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
017816,000349: 
017817,000350:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
017818,000351:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
017819,000352:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
017820,000353:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
017821,000354:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
017822,000355:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
017823,000356: 
017824,000357:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
017825,000358:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1    11       ALL ARE OCTAL
017826,000359:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2    10
017827,000360:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3    7
017828,000361:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4    6
017829,000362:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5    5
017830,000363:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1    4
017831,000364:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2    3
017832,000365:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3    2
017833,000366:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4    1
017834,000367:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5    0
017835,000368:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
017836,000369: 
017837,000370: 
017838,000371:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
017839,000372: 
017840,000373:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
017841,000374:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
017842,000375:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
017843,000376:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
017844,000377:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
017845,000378:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)

Page 409 

017847,000380:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
017848,000381:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
017849,000382:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
017850,000383:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
017851,000384:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
017852,000385:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
017853,000386:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
017854,000387:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
017855,000388: 
017856,000389: 
017857,000390:                                                                                                  #  THE 5-BIT OUTOUT RELAY CODES ARE:
017858,000391:                                                                                                  #  BLANK      00000
017859,000392:                                                                                                  #  0          10101
017860,000393:                                                                                                  #  1          00011
017861,000394:                                                                                                  #  2          11001
017862,000395:                                                                                                  #  3          11011
017863,000396:                                                                                                  #  4          01111
017864,000397:                                                                                                  #  5          11110
017865,000398:                                                                                                  #  6          11100
017866,000399:                                                                                                  #  7          10011
017867,000400:                                                                                                  #  8          11101
017868,000401:                                                                                                  #  9          11111
017869,000402:

018589,001122:

Page 426 

018591,001124:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
018592,001125:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
018593,001126:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
018594,001127:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
018595,001128:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
018596,001129:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
018597,001130: 
018598,001131:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
018599,001132:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
018600,001133: 
018601,001134:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
018602,001135: 
018603,001136:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
018604,001137:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
018605,001138:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
018606,001139: 
018607,001140:                                                                                                  #  MIXED-CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018608,001141:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
018609,001142:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018610,001143:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018611,001144:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018612,001145:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
018613,001146: 
018614,001147:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
018615,001148:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
018616,001149:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
018617,001150:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
018618,001151:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
018619,001152: 
018620,001153:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
018621,001154:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
018622,001155:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
018623,001156:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018624,001157:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
018625,001158:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018626,001159:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018627,001160:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018628,001161: 
018629,001162: 
018630,001163:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
018631,001164:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
018632,001165:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
018633,001166: 
018634,001167: 
018635,001168:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
018636,001169:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
018637,001170: 
018638,001171:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
018639,001172:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
018640,001173:

Page 427 

018642,001175:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY  VERBS
018643,001176: 41,2402           44743        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
018644,001177: 41,2403           02453                           TC       COMPTEST

019243,001776:                                                                                                  #  DETECTED DURING ENTER OF DATA, CHECK FAIL IS TURNED ON AND IT RECYCLES
019244,001777:                                                                                                  #  TO EXECUTE  OF ORIGINAL LOAD VERB. RECYCLE CAUSED BY  1) DECIMAL MACHINE
019245,001778:                                                                                                  #  CADR  2) MIXTURE OF OCTAL/DECIMAL DATA  3) OCTAL DATA INTO DECIMAL
019246,001779:                                                                                                  #  ONLY NOUN  4) DEC DATA INTO OCT ONLY NOUN  5) DATA TOO LARGE FOR SCALE
019247,001780:                                                                                                  #  6) FEWER THAN 3 DATA WORDS LOADED FOR HRS, MIN, SEC NOUN.8(2)-(6) ALARM

019854,002387: 42,3617                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
019855,002388:

Page 452 

019857,002390:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
019858,002391:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
019859,002392:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
019860,002393:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
019861,002394:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
019862,002395: 
019863,002396:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
019864,002397:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
019865,002398:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
019866,002399:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
019867,002400:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
019868,002401:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
019869,002402:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
019870,002403: 
019871,002404:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON(+=ON, +0=OFF)
019872,002405:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019873,002406:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019874,002407: 
019875,002408:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
019876,002409:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
019877,002410: 
019878,002411:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
019879,002412:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
019880,002413: 
019881,002414:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOESNT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW.
019882,002415: 41,3302                                           SETLOC   ENDRUTIN                              
019883,002416: 
019884,002417: 41,3302                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019885,002418: 41,3302           43311        MONITOR            CS       BIT15/14                              
019886,002419: 41,3303           71016                           MASK     NOUNCADR                              
019887,002420: 41,3304           54155        MONIT1             TS       MPAC       +1                         #  TEMP STORAGE

020009,002542:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
020010,002543:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
020011,002544:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F ( FCADR 4000-7777)
020012,002545: 
020013,002546:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
020014,002547: 
020015,002548:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
020016,002549:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
020017,002550:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
020018,002551: 
020019,002552:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
020020,002553:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
020021,002554:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
020022,002555: 
020023,002556: 41,3425           34310        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
020024,002557: 41,3426           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
020025,002558: 41,3427           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
020026,002559: 41,3430           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
020027,002560: 41,3431           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
020028,002561: 41,3432           04642                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.

020460,002993:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
020461,002994:

Page 465 

020463,002996:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
020464,002997: 
020465,002998:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
020466,002999: 
020467,003000:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
020468,003001:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
020469,003002:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
020470,003003:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
020471,003004: 
020472,003005:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
020473,003006:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
020474,003007:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
020475,003008: 
020476,003009:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
020477,003010:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
020478,003011:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
020479,003012:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
020480,003013:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
020481,003014:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
020482,003015:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
020483,003016:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
020484,003017:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
020485,003018:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
020486,003019:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
020487,003020: 
020488,003021: 40,3517           44742        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
020489,003022: 40,3520           00006                           EXTEND                                         
020490,003023: 40,3521           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OF UPACT LITE
020491,003024: 40,3522           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
020492,003025: 40,3523           34727                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020493,003026: 40,3524           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
020494,003027: 40,3525           10000                           CCS      A                                     
020495,003028: 40,3526           03535                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
020496,003029: 40,3527           04450        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
020497,003030: 40,3530           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
020498,003031: 40,3531           03533                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
020499,003032: 40,3532           05146                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020500,003033: 40,3533           04626                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
020501,003034: 40,3534           21062                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
020502,003035: 40,3535           34746        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
020503,003036: 40,3536           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
020504,003037: 40,3537           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
020505,003038: 40,3540           05146                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
020506,003039: 40,3541           04473                           TC       RELDSP1                               
020507,003040: 40,3542           05146                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020508,003041: 
020509,003042: 40,3543                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
020510,003043:

Page 466 

020512,003045:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
020513,003046:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
020514,003047:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
020515,003048:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
020516,003049:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
020517,003050: 
020518,003051:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WTIH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
020519,003052:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
020520,003053:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
020521,003054: 
020522,003055:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WTIH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
020523,003056:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
020524,003057: 
020525,003058:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020526,003059:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAIALBLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
020527,003060:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
020528,003061:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
020529,003062:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
020530,003063: 
020531,003064:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020532,003065:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
020533,003066:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
020534,003067:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
020535,003068: 
020536,003069:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
020537,003070:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
020538,003071:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
020539,003072:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
020540,003073:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
020541,003074:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
020542,003075:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
020543,003076: 
020544,003077:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
020545,003078:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
020546,003079: 
020547,003080:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
020548,003081:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
020549,003082: 
020550,003083:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
020551,003084:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
020552,003085: 
020553,003086:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
020554,003087:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
020555,003088:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
020556,003089:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
020557,003090:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WTIH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
020558,003091:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
020559,003092:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
020560,003093: 
020561,003094:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 461 

020563,003096:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
020564,003097:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASED INT THE VERB
020565,003098:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
020566,003099:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
020567,003100:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
020568,003101:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
020569,003102:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
020570,003103:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
020571,003104:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
020572,003105: 
020573,003106:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
020574,003107:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
020575,003108: 
020576,003109:    4145                                           SETLOC   MID7       +1                         
020577,003110:    4145                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020578,003111:    4145           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
020579,003112:    4146           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP

020585,003118:    4154           34744                           CAF      ONE                                   #  DSP SYST AVAILABLE
020586,003119:    4155           60002        NVSBCOM            AD       Q
