020681,003214:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS ).
020682,003215: 
020683,003216:    4175                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
020684,003217:    4175                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020685,003218:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
020686,003219:    4175           34726        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
020687,003220:    4176           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
020688,003221:                                                                                                  #   MONITOR BIT.
020689,003222:    4177           00002                           TC       Q                                     
020690,003223: 
020691,003224: 
020692,003225:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
020693,003226:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020694,003227:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020695,003228:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
020696,003229:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
020697,003230: 
020698,003231: 
020699,003232:                                                                                                  #  L  TC ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
020700,003233:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
020701,003234:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
020702,003235:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020703,003236:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020704,003237:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
020705,003238:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
020706,003239:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
020707,003240:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
020708,003241:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
020709,003242: 
020710,003243: 
020711,003244:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
020712,003245:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
020713,003246:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS

Page 470 

020715,003248:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020716,003249:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
020717,003250:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
020718,003251: 
020719,003252:    4200           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
020720,003253:    4201           04211                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
020721,003254:    4202           04215                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
020722,003255:    4203           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
020723,003256:    4204           75003                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
020724,003257:    4205           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
020725,003258:    4206           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
020726,003259:    4207           05124                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020727,003260: 
020728,003261: 
020729,003262:    4210           05146        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020730,003263: 
020731,003264: 
020732,003265:    4211           11041        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
020733,003266:    4212           04220                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

020774,003307: 
020775,003308: 
020776,003309:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
020777,003310:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
020778,003311:                                                                                                  #  BIT1=1 BLANKS R1, BIT2=1 BLANKS R2, BIT3=1 BLANKS R3.
020779,003312:                                                                                                  #  ANY COMBINATION OF THESE BITS IS ACCEPTED.
020780,003313: 
020781,003314:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT IS RESTORED TO STATE IT WAS IN BEFORE BLANKSUB WAS EXECUTED.
020782,003315:

020785,003318:    4250           34727                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020786,003319:    4251           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT

Page 478 

021068,003601:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
021069,003602: 
021070,003603:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
021071,003604:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
021072,003605:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
021073,003606:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
021074,003607: 
021075,003608:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021076,003609:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
021077,003610:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
021078,003611:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
021079,003612:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021080,003613:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
021081,003614:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
021082,003615: 
021083,003616: 
021084,003617:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
021085,003618:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
021086,003619:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
021087,003620:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
021088,003621:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
021089,003622: 
021090,003623: 
021091,003624:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
021092,003625:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021093,003626:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
021094,003627:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
021095,003628:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
021096,003629: 
021097,003630: 
021098,003631:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
021099,003632:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
021100,003633:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
021101,003634: 
021102,003635: 
021103,003636:                                                                                                  #  .
021104,003637: 
021105,003638: 
021106,003639:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
021107,003640:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
021108,003641:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL
021109,003642:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
021110,003643: 
021111,003644: 
021112,003645:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021113,003646:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
021114,003647:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
021115,003648:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY FO THE DSPLIST
021116,003649:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
021117,003650:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 479 

021119,003652:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
021120,003653: 
021121,003654:    4430           44435        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED

021140,003673: 
021141,003674: 
021142,003675:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
021143,003676:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
021144,003677:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
021145,003678:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
021146,003679:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.

021158,003691:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.

021160,003693:    4447           14430                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
